          <!-- Sign Up Widget CSS -->
          <style type="text/css">
           #sign-up-wdgt {

         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
          <!-- Sign Up Widget JS -->
          <script>
           window.onload = function () {
        console.log('widget loaded');
        var reactwait = setInterval(function () {
            if ($('#sign-up-wdgt').length != 0 || undefined) {
                clearInterval(reactwait);    
                $('a.toggle-open, a.rkd-sw-close-btn').show();            
                $('#sign-up-wdgt').css('opacity', '1');            
                var mainSticky = $('#sign-up-wdgt'),
                    plusBtn = $('a.rkd-sw-plus-wrapper'),
                    closeBtn = $('a.rkd-sw-close-btn'),
                    toggleOpen = $('a.toggle-open'),
                    envelopeOn = $('.envelope-container');
                $('a.toggle-open, a.rkd-sw-plus-wrapper, a.rkd-sw-close-btn').on('click', function(e){
                    e.preventDefault();
                    if (mainSticky.hasClass('open')) {
                        mainSticky.removeClass('open');
                        mainSticky.addClass('closed');
                        mainSticky.css('opacity','0');
                        closeBtn.hide();
                        plusBtn.show();
                        hideBackground();
                    } else {
                        mainSticky.addClass('open');
                        mainSticky.removeClass('closed');
                        mainSticky.css('opacity','1');
                        closeBtn.show();
                        plusBtn.hide();
                        hideBackground();
                    }
                });
                function hideBackground() {
                    mainSticky.hasClass('open') ? toggleOpen.css({'box-shadow': 'none', 'background': 'transparent'}) : toggleOpen.css({'box-shadow': 'inherit','background' : 'rgba(234,69,37,0.85)'});
                }
            }
        }, 100);
    }
          </script>

         <div class="wpb_wrapper">
          <script type="text/javascript">
           var reactwait = setInterval(function(){ 
    if(document.querySelectorAll(".cta_save_a_life").length > 0){
        clearInterval(reactwait);
        //console.log("loading...");
        var giftArray  = document.querySelectorAll(".gift_array");
        var button = document.getElementById("cta_save_a_life");
        var other = document.getElementById("cta_other_amount");
        var url = "https://secure.madd.org/page/22522/donate/1?transaction.donationAmt=";
        button.addEventListener("click", function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
            //console.log("Click");
            if(other.value != "" && parseInt(other.value) > 0){
                //console.log("value:" + other.value)
                var newUrl ="";
                newUrl= url+other.value;
                //console.log("url:" + newUrl)
                window.open(newUrl, '_self');
            }
        });
        giftArray.forEach(function(ga){
            ga.addEventListener("click", function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                document.getElementById("cta_other_amount").value = this.id;
                console.log("click...");
                var x = parseInt(this.id);
                onChangeOther(x);    
            });
        });
        document.querySelector("#cta_other_amount").addEventListener("change",function(){
            console.log("change...");
            var x = parseInt(this.value);
            onChangeOther(x);
        })
        document.querySelector("#cta_other_amount").addEventListener("keyup",function(){
            console.log("keyup...");
            var x = parseInt(this.value);
            onChangeOther(x);        
        })
    }
},10);
function onChangeOther(x){
    
    if(x != NaN && x > 0){
        document.querySelector(".cta_ga > span.left").classList.add("input-dollar");
    }else{
        document.querySelector(".cta_ga > span.left").classList.remove("input-dollar");
    }
}
          </script>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
